)||lowerStr.includes('pago')){isPaid=true;const inMatch=str.match(/In:\$([\d.]+)/);const outMatch=str.match(/Out:\$([\d.]+)/);const inCost=inMatch?parseFloat(inMatch[1]):0;const if (dropFromHigh > limitDrop) continue; trendStr = "Desplome"; } results.push({ ticker: row.ticker, name: row.name, price: parseFloat(row.price.toFixed(2)), trendStatus: trendStr, per: row.per ? parseFloat(row.per.toFixed(2)) : "N/A", peg: row.peg ? parseFloat(row.peg.toFixed(2)) : "N/A", roi: row.roi ? parseFloat(row.roi.toFixed(2)) : "N/A", divYield: row.divYield ? parseFloat(row.divYield.toFixed(2)) : "N/A", pb: row.pb ? parseFloat(row.pb.toFixed(2)) : "N/A", debtEquity: row.de ? parseFloat((row.de/100).toFixed(2)) : "N/A", fcf: row.fcf ? parseFloat(row.fcf.toFixed(2)) : "N/A", epsGrowth: row.epsGrowth ? parseFloat(row.epsGrowth.toFixed(2)) : "N/A" }); } } function fetchStockData(tickersString) { var tickerList = tickersString.split(","); var requests = []; var validTickers = []; var yahooSymbols = []; for (var i = 0; i < tickerList.length; i++) { var rawTicker = tickerList[i].trim(); }); if (closes.length >= 2) { p = closes[closes.length - 1]; // Último precio real registrado pc = closes[closes.length - 2]; // Cierre de la sesión de bolsa inmediatamente anterior } else if (closes.length === 1) { p = closes[0]; } return ContentService.createTextOutput(JSON.stringify(results)).setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JSON); } function convertToYahoo(rawTicker) { if (!rawTicker || typeof rawTicker !== 'string') { return ""; } var indexMap = { "INDEXSP:.INX": "^GSPC", "INDEXDJX:.DJI": "^DJI", "INDEXNASDAQ:.IXIC":"^IXIC", "INDEXRUSSELL:RUT": "^RUT", "INDEXCBOE:VIX": "^VIX", "INDEXFTSE:UKX": "^FTSE", "INDEXEURO:SX5E": "^STOXX50E", "BME:IBEX": "^IBEX", "INDEXBVB:BET": "^BET" }; } function fetchFundamentalData(rawTicker) { if (!rawTicker) { return ContentService.createTextOutput(JSON.stringify({ success: false, error: "Error: No se ha proporcionado un ticker válido para la consulta." })).setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JSON); calculateFIFODetail=(p,qtyToSell)=>{const fDateEU=d=>d?d.split('-').reverse().join('-'):'';const r2=n=>Math.round((parseFloat(n)||0)*100)/100;const r6=n=>Math.round((parseFloat(n)||0)*1000000)/1000000;let lots=p.lots&&p.lots.length>0?JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(p.lots)):[{id:Date.now(),date:p.buyDate,shares:p.shares,price:p.buyPrice,fx:p.buyFx,fees:p.fees,adj:p.adjustments,pe:p.buyPE}];lots.sort((a,b)=>new Date(a.date)-new Date(b.date));let remainingToSell=qtyToSell;let ext={shares:0,costBase:0,costFx:0,fees:0,adj:0,weightedTime:0,desc:[],consumedLots:[]};let newLots=[];lots.forEach(lot=>{const lS=parseFloat(lot.shares)||0;const lP=parseFloat(lot.price)||0;const lF=parseFloat(lot.fx)||1;if(remainingToSell<=0){newLots.push(lot);return;}const take=Math.min(lS,remainingToSell);const ratio=take/lS;ext.shares+=take;ext.costBase+=take*lP;ext.costFx+=take*lP*lF;ext.fees=r2(ext.fees+lot.fees*ratio);ext.adj=r2(ext.adj+lot.adj*ratio);ext.weightedTime+=new Date(lot.date).getTime()*take;ext.desc.push(`• ${formatN(take)} acc. del ${fDateEU(lot.date)} [P: ${formatN(lP,3)} | FX: ${formatN(lF,4)} | Gtos: ${formatN(r2(lot.fees*ratio)+r2(lot.adj*ratio))}]`);ext.consumedLots.push({...lot,shares:take,fees:r2(lot.fees*ratio),adj:r2(lot.adj*ratio)});if(lS>take){newLots.push({...lot,shares:r6(lS-take),fees:r2(lot.fees*(1-ratio)),adj:r2(lot.adj*(1-ratio))});}remainingToSell-=take;});return{extracted:{shares:r6(ext.shares),buyPrice:r6(ext.costBase/ext.shares),buyFx:r6(ext.costFx/ext.costBase),buyDate:new Date(ext.weightedTime/ext.shares).toISOString().split('T')[0],buyDateEU:fDateEU(new Date(ext.weightedTime/ext.shares).toISOString().split('T')[0]),fees:r2(ext.fees),adj:r2(ext.adj),summary:"\n"+ext.desc.join('\n'),consumedLots:ext.consumedLots},remainingLots:newLots};};const const UtilsTab=({baseCurrency,customLinks=[],setCustomLinks})=>{const[activeSubTab,setActiveSubTab]=useState('links');// --- 1. CALCULADORA DE INTERÉS COMPUESTO (Corregido con lógica Bagger de Retorno) --- const CompoundCalculator=()=>{const[compState,setCompState]=usePersistentState('bg_compoundCalc',{principal:10000,annualAddition:6000,years:20,rate:10,inflationRate:2.5,compoundsPerYear:1,addAtStart:true});const[showCompTable,setShowCompTable]=useState(false);const calculateCompound=()=>{let balance=compState.principal;let totalPrincipal=compState.principal;const history=[];let crossoverYear=null;const r=compState.rate/100;const inf=(compState.inflationRate||0)/100;const n=compState.compoundsPerYear;const effectiveAnnualRate=Math.pow(1+r/n,n)-1;let lastBagger=0;// Iniciamos en 0 (menos del 100% de retorno) const baggers=[];for(let i=1;i<=compState.years;i++){let contribution=compState.annualAddition;if(compState.addAtStart){balance+=contribution;totalPrincipal+=contribution;}const interestEarned=balance*effectiveAnnualRate;balance+=interestEarned;if(!compState.addAtStart){balance+=contribution;totalPrincipal+=contribution;}const currentInterest=balance-totalPrincipal;if(crossoverYear===null&¤tInterest>totalPrincipal){crossoverYear=i;}const currentBagger=totalPrincipal>0?Math.floor(currentInterest/totalPrincipal):0;const yearBaggers=[];if(currentBagger>lastBagger){for(let b=lastBagger+1;b<=currentBagger;b++){baggers.push({year:i,level:b});yearBaggers.push(b);}lastBagger=currentBagger;}const realBalance=balance/Math.pow(1+inf,i);history.push({year:i,principal:totalPrincipal,interest:currentInterest,balance:balance,realBalance:realBalance,yearBaggers:yearBaggers});}const finalRealBalance=balance/Math.pow(1+inf,compState.years);return{finalBalance:balance,finalRealBalance,totalPrincipal,history,crossoverYear,baggers};};const compResult=calculateCompound();const handleCompChange=(k,v)=>setCompState(p=>({...p,[k]:parseFloat(v)||0}));return/*#__PURE__*/_jsxDEV("div",{className:"max-w-5xl mx-auto space-y-6 fade-in font-bold text-green-400 mb-8 flex items-center gap-3",children:[/*#__PURE__*/_jsxDEV(Icons.TrendingUp,{className:"w-8 h-8"},void 0,false)," Interés Compuesto Ajustado a Inflación"]},void 0,true),/*#__PURE__*/_jsxDEV("div",{className:"grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-5 gap-6
